# HTML Notes/Bangla Documentation

 - ##  Html ‡¶ï‡¶ø? 
    HTML ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **‚ÄúHyper Text Markup Language‚Äù**. HTML ‡¶π‡¶≤ Web Pages ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂ Markup Language. HTML ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ HTML ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø Browser ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Content ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

- ##  Html ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨?
    
    HTML ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Web Document ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Structure ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ HTML ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ Web Language ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Browser ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶≤ Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Common use ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É- 
    
    - Web Page Structure ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
    - Web Page Navigation ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé Web ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï Page ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Link ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
    - Web Page ‡¶è Images ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Videos Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§
- ##  Html Tag ‡¶ï‡¶ø? Html Tag ‡¶ï‡ßü ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø?
    
    HTML Tag ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Keywords ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨ Browser ‡¶ï‡ßá Web Page ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Format ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∏‡¶¨ Tag ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Open Tag, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Close Tag. Some HTML Tag: 
    
    ```html
    <html>  => Opening Tag
    </html> => Closing Tag
    <h1> </h1>  - Heading Tag ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Heading ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
    <p> </p>    - Paragraph Tag ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ paragraph ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
    <b> </b>    - Bold Tag ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ text ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
    <u> </u>    - Underline Tag ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ text underline ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
    ```
    
    **`<h1>`** ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá **`<h6>`** ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡ß¨‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML Heading Tag ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Website ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Titles ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ Subtitles ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ Search Engines Heading ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Content Index ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§  Example:
    
    ```html
    <h1>Heading 1</h1>
    <h2>Heading 2</h2>
    <h3>Heading 3</h3>
    <h4>Heading 4</h4>
    <h5>Heading 5</h5>
    <h6>Heading 6</h6>
    ```
    
    HTML Tag ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤:
    
    - Container Tag,
    - Empty Tag ‡¶¨‡¶æ Void Tag.
    
    <ins>***Container Tag***</ins> :
    
    ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ Opening ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Closing ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Tag ‡¶ï‡ßá Container Tag ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® **`<b>content...</b>`**
    
    <ins>***Empty Tag***</ins> ‡¶¨‡¶æ <ins>***Void Tag***</ins> :
    
    ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ Opening Tag ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Tag ‡¶ï‡ßá Empty Tag ‡¶¨‡¶æ Void Tag ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®, **`<br/>`** , **`<hr/>`**
    
    ### <ins>*HTML Meta Tags ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤*</ins> :
    
    **`<!DOCTYPE>`**, **`<title>`**, **`<link>`**, **`<meta>`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`<style>`**
    
    ### <ins>*HTML Text Tags ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤*</ins> :
    
    **`<p>`**, **`<h1>`**, **`<h2>`**, **`<h3>`**, **`<h4>`**, **`<h5>`**, **`<h6>`**,**`<b>`**, **`<strong>`**,**`<i>`**, **`<u>`**, **`<em>`**, **`<abbr>`**, **`<address>`**, **`<bdo>`**, **`<blockquote>`**, **`<cite>`**, **`<q>`**, **`<code>`**, **`<ins>`**, **`<del>`**, **`<pre>`**,**`<small>`**, **`<samp>`**, **`<var>`** ,**`<hr>`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`<br>`**
    
    ### <ins>*HTML Link Tags ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤*</ins> :
    
    **`<a>`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`<base>`**
    
    ### <ins>*HTML Image and Object Tags ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤*</i> :
  
    **`<img>`**, **`<map>`**,**`<area>`**,**`<picture>`**, **`<source>`**, **`<param>`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`<object>`**
    
    ### <ins> *HTML List Tags ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤* </i> :
    
    **`<ul>`**, **`<ol>`**, **`<li>`**, **`<dl>`**, **`<dt>`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`<dd>`**
    
    ### <ins> *HTML Table Tags ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤* </i> :
    
    **`<table>`**, **`<tr>`**, **`<td>`**, **`<th>`**, **`<tbody>`**, **`<thead>`**, **`<tfoot>`**, **`<col>`**, **`<colgroup>`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`<caption>`**
    
    ### <ins> *HTML Form Tags ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤* </i> :
    
    **`<form>`**, **`<input>`**, **`<textarea>`**, **`<select>`**, **`<option>`**, **`<optgroup>`**, **`<button>`**, **`<label>`**, **`<progress>`**, **`<fieldset>`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`<legend>`**
    
    ### <ins> *HTML Scripting Tags ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤* </ins> :
    
    **`<script>`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`<noscript>`**
    
    ---
    
- ## Html  Element ‡¶ï‡¶ø? Html Element ‡¶ï‡ßü ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø?
    
    HTML element ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Starting Tag ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Content ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá Ending Tag ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶•‡¶æ, HTML Element ‡¶π‡¶≤ Start Tag ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Close Tag ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡•§ Ex: 
    
    ```html
    <h1> Hello world </h1>  - ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML Element.
    ```
    
    ***Nested HTML Elements:***¬†HTML Element Nested ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Element ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
    
    Default Display ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç styling Purpose ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá HTML Element ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á categories ‡¶è ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤: 
    
    - Block-level element
    - Inline element
    
    ### *Block-level element*:
    
    Block-level Element ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶¨ Element ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Block-level Element ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Line ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Block-level Element ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
      </head>
      <body>
        <div style="background-color: lightblue">This is first div</div>
        <div style="background-color: lightgreen">This is second div</div>
        <p style="background-color: pink">This is a block level element</p>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Block-level Element ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø CSS Property **`background-color`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ CSS Notes ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§
    
    HTML ‡¶è Block-level Element ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤:
    
        <address>, <article>, <aside>, <blockquote>, <canvas>, <dd>, <div>, <dl>, <dt>, <fieldset>, <figcaption>, <figure>, <footer>, <form>, <h1> - <h6>, <header>, <hr>, <li>, <main>, <nav>, <noscript>, <ol>, <output>, <p>, <pre>, <section>, <table>, <tfoot>, <ul> and <video>.
    
    ### ***Inline elements***:
    
    Inline Element ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶¨ Element ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Inline Element ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Inline Element ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Line ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§ Inline Element ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
    
    Example:
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
      </head>
      <body>
         <a href="https://www.javatpoint.com/html-tutorial">Click on link</a>
         <span style="background-color: lightblue">this is inline element</span>
         <p>This will take the width of the text only</p>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    HTML ‡¶è Inline Element ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤:
    
        <a>, <abbr>, <acronym>, <b>, <bdo>, <big>, <br>, <button>, <cite>, <code>, <dfn>, <em>, <i>, <img>, <input>, <kbd>, <label>, <map>, <object>, <q>, <samp>, <script>, <select>, <small>, <span>, <strong>, <sub>, <sup>, <textarea>, <time>, <tt>, <var>.
    
    ---
    
- ## Html Attribute ‡¶ï‡¶ø? ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Attribute ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶¨?
    
    HTML-‡¶è, Attributes ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü HTML Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Behavior ‡¶¨‡¶æ Appearance ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶π ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ Attributes ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü Opening Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡•§ Attribute ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Name ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Value ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶π‡ßç‡¶® (=) ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Value ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÉ‡¶•‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç (") ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶π‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Attribute ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü **`<Tag_Name Attribute_Name = "Value"> Content </Tag_Name>`**
    
    ```html
    <a href="https://www.example.com">Click here</a>  
    Here **herf** is Attribute Name and **https://www.example.com** is Attribute Value.
    ```
    
    **Some common attributes are:** 
    
    - **`class :`**  ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï CSS  ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∏ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ CSS Style ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§
    - **`id:`** ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Unique Identifier ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá CSS Style ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Content ‡¶ï‡ßá Manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    - **`src:`** ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ HTML Document ‡¶è‡¶∞ Image, Video Or Audio File ‡¶è‡¶∞ URL Source ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ß∑
    - **`alt:`** ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ HTML Document ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Image Or Video File load ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® Alternative Text ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Image  File ‡¶¨‡¶æ Video File ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø load ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Text ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø Alternative  ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá,  ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡•§
    - **`style:`** ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ HTML Document ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Inline CSS ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø Apply ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    - **`disabled:`** ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Button, From Element, Input Field, User Interaction ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    - **`placeholder:`** ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Input Field ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ Short Hint Or Example Text ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶≤ HTML Attributes ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨ Attributes Set ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Element's ‡¶è‡¶∞ Functionality ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Different Purposes ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® Purpose ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
    
    ### <ins>*The Lang Attribute*</ins> :
    
    Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Language Declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ **`<html>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá **`lang`** Attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ö ‡¶á‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá Language ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶®‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶ü‡¶ø Language ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá English ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html lang="en">
    <body>
    ...
    </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`lang`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Language Code ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø Country Codes ‡¶ì Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ø Characters Define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Language ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ø Characters Define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Country Code ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶®‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶ü‡¶ø Language ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá English ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Country ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá United States ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html lang="en-US">
    <body>
    ...
    </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    > [Visit this link for All HTML¬†Language Code¬†Reference.](https://www.w3schools.com/tags/ref_language_codes.asp)
    > 
    
    > [Visit this link for All HTML¬†ISO Country Codes¬†Reference.](https://www.w3schools.com/tags/ref_country_codes.asp)
    > 
    
    ---
    
- ## Web Browser ‡¶ï‡¶ø? ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?
    
    Web Browser ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Application Software ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Web Pages ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Text, Image, Video, Animation, Form ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ Data, Server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Web Page ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Navigate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Interface ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ Input ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Browser ‡¶∏‡¶ö‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤: Chrome, Firefox, Microsoft Edge, Opera ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Web Browser ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá:
    
    1. ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø URL (Web Address) Enter ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø Web Server ‡¶è Request ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
    2. Server ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Data ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶®‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡ßá‡•§
    3. HTML, CSS ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç JavaScript Code ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá Render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Web Page ‡¶è Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
    4. ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Media Data ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Image, Video, Animation ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø Load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
    5. User ‡¶è‡¶∞ Input ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Click, Keyboard Event ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶∞ Appropriate Response ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
    6. Web Page ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Navigation Tools ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Link ‡¶è Click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Web Page ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ, History Management ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ, Back Button, Refresh Button ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ  Html Document ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ Basic Structure ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø?
    
    ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá Computer ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ (*Desktop, C/D/E ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Drive ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ Drive ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Folder ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞* ) Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø New File ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® File ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Name ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá File ‡¶è‡¶∞ Extension ‡¶ü‡¶æ Change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá html ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ 
    
     Html File ‡¶è Document ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Structure ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML File ‡¶è‡¶á Structure ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Structure ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡•§
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
        <title>Page Title</title>
      </head>
      <body>
        <h1>My First Heading</h1>
        <p>My first paragraph.</p>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    - ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`<!DOCTYPE html>`** ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Browser ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ File Load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ **`<!DOCTYPE html>`** ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Browser ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á File ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML5 Document.
    - HTML Document ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡ßü **`<html>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡ßü **`</html>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Root Element.
    - **`<head>`** Element ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá HTML Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Meta Information ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    - **`<title>`** Element ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ HTML Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Title ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶á Title ‡¶ü‡¶ø Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ Title Bar Or Page Tab ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
    - **`<body>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá HTML Document ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ Body. ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Container ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Visible Contents ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® headings, paragraphs, images, hyperlinks, tables, lists, etc.
    
    ### ***HTML Page Structure:***
    
    ![HTML Page Structure.png](./document-Images/HTML_Page_Structure.png)
    
    
   > üí° <ins>***Note:***</ins> Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ **`<body>`** Element ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ index.html ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá File ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá By Default Show ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶®  ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á , Html Formatting Element ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?
    
    HTML **`<b>`** and **`<strong>`** ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ø Element ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á‡¶Æ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Text ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡ßÅ ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE>
    <html>  
      <body>  
           <b> Bold text </b> <br>  
           <strong> Important text </strong> 
      </body>  
    </html>
    
    ```
    
    HTML **`<i>`** and **`<em>`** ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ø Element ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á‡¶Æ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Text ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡ßÅ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Å‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    
    ```html
    
    <!DOCTYPE>
    <html>  
      <body>  
         <i> Italic text </i> <br>
         <em> Emphasized text</em>  
      </body>  
    </html>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<small>`** Element  ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE>
    <html>  
      <body>  
         <p> This is Normal Text </p>
         <small> This is some smaller text </small>   
      </body>  
    </html>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<mark>`** Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Highlight ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE>
    <html>  
      <body>  
          <p> Do not forget to buy <mark> milk </mark> today.</p>
      </body>  
    </html>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<del>`** Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Document ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Delete ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá Browser ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ Text  ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶Å‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§ 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE>
    <html>  
      <body>  
          <p>My favorite color is <del>blue</del> red.</p>
      </body>  
    </html>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<u>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá Underline ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE>
    <html>  
      <body>  
           <p> Write Your First <u>Paragraph</u> in underlined text.</p>   
      </body>  
    </html>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<ins>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá HTML Document ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Text Inserted ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Browser Inserted Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá Underline ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <body>
         <p>My favorite color is <del>blue</del> <ins>red</ins>.</p>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<sub>`** Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Text ‡¶ï‡ßá Subscript ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Normal Line ‡¶è‡¶∞ Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶´ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Chemical Formula ‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE>
    <html>  
      <body>  
          <p>This is <sub>subscripted</sub> text.</p>
          <p>Water Symbol is H<sub>2</sub>O</p>
      </body>  
    </html>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<sup>`** Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Text ‡¶ï‡ßá Superscript ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Normal Line ‡¶è‡¶∞ Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶´ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Footnotes, Mathematical Formula ‡¶§‡ßá‡•§
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE>
    <html>  
      <body>  
          <p>This is <sup>superscripted</sup> text.</p>
          <p> (a+b)<sup>2</sup> = a<sup>2</sup> + 2ab + b<sup>2</sup> </p>
      </body>  
    </html>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<pre>`** Element ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
      <!DOCTYPE html>
      <html>
        <body>
            <p>The pre tag preserves both spaces and line breaks:</p>
            <pre>
              My Bonnie lies over the ocean.
            
              My Bonnie lies over the sea.
            
              My Bonnie lies over the ocean.
              
              Oh, bring back my Bonnie to me.
            </pre>
        </body>
      </html>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<br>`** Tag Use  ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Line Break ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Current Text Line ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Next Line ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Example
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
      </head>
      <body>
        <p>This is First Line. This is second Line </p>  <!--Without br Tag -->
        
        <p>This is First Line. <br> This is second Line </p> <!--With br Tag -->
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<hr>`** Tag Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Website ‡¶è Horizontal Line Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
      </head>
      <body>
        <h1>This is Hedding </h1> 
        <hr>
        <p>Lorem Ipsum is simply dummy text of the printing and typesetting industry. Lorem Ipsum has been the industry's standard dummy text ever since the 1500s, when an unknown printer took a galley of type and scrambled it to make a type specimen book.</p>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<kbd>`** Tag ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Keyboard ‡¶è‡¶∞ Input Define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Website ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® keyboard Shortcut ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<body>
    		<h1>The kbd element</h1>
    		<p>Press <kbd>Ctrl</kbd> + <kbd>C</kbd> to copy text (Windows).</p>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<code>`** Tag ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Computer Code ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßá Define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Website ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Programming Code ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    <body>
      <h2>The code Element</h2>
      <p>Programming code example:</p>
      <code>
        x = 5;
        y = 6;
        z = x + y;
      </code>

      <h2>The code Element with pre tag</h2>
      <pre>
        <code>
          x = 5;
          y = 6;
          z = x + y;
        </code>
      </pre>
    </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    
   > üí° <ins>***Note:***</ins>  **`<code>`** Tag ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ Space ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Line Break ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶¨ ‡¶ì‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶´‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`<pre>`** Tag ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
  
    
    HTML **`<samp>`** Tag ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Computer Code ‡¶è‡¶∞ Output ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßá Define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<body>
    		<h2>The samp Element</h2>
    		<p>Message from my computer:</p>
    		<p><samp>File not found.<br>Press F1 to continue</samp></p>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<var>`** Tag ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Computer Programming ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ Mathematical Expression ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Variable Define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<body>
    		<h2>The var Element</h2>
    		<p>The area of a triangle is: 1/2 x <var>b</var> x <var>h</var>, where <var>b</var> is the base, and <var>h</var> is the vertical height.</p>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶®  ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á , Html Quotations Element ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã  ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?
    
    HTML **`<blockquote>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Web Site ‡¶è, Another Web Site ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®  Text ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ Source ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ **`cite`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Source ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<body>
    			<p>Here is a quote from WWF's website:</p>
    			<blockquote cite="http://www.worldwildlife.org/who/index.html">
    			      For 60 years, WWF has worked to help people and nature thrive. As the world's leading conservation organization, WWF works in nearly 100 countries. At every level, we collaborate with people around the world to develop and deliver innovative solutions that protect communities, wildlife, and the places in which they live.
    			</blockquote>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<q>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ HTML Element Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Quotation Mark ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <body>
    	   <p>Browsers usually insert quotation marks around the q element.</p>
    	   <p>WWF's goal is to: <q>Build a future where people live in harmony with nature.</q></p>
     </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<abbr>`** Element ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Abbreviation Word(like HTML, CSS, Dr. ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ Text ‡¶ï‡ßá Title ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`title`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ Text ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<body>
    			<p>The <abbr title="World Health Organization">WHO</abbr> was founded in 1948.</p>
    			<p>Marking up abbreviations can give useful information to browsers, translation systems and search-engines.</p>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<address>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Document ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ Article Owner ‡¶è‡¶∞ Contact Information ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Contact Information ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá Email Address, URL, Physical Address, Phone Number, Social Media ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<body>
    			<p>The HTML address element defines contact information (author/owner) of a document or article.</p>
    			<address>
    				Written by John Doe.<br> 
    				Visit us at:<br>
    				Example.com<br>
    				Box 564, Disneyland<br>
    				USA
    			</address>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<cite>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Creative Work(a book, a painting, a song ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø) ‡¶è‡¶∞ Title ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Browser ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ cite Element text ‡¶ï‡ßá Italic ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§ Example:  
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<body>
    			<p>The HTML cite element defines the title of a work.</p>
    			<p>Browsers usually display cite elements in italic.</p>
    			<img src="./img_the_scream.jpg" width="220" height="277" alt="The Scream">
    			<p><cite>The Scream</cite> by Edvard Munch. Painted in 1893.</p>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    > üí° <ins>***Note:***</ins> ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶®  ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á , Html Comment ‡¶ï‡¶ø? ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü?
    
    Comment ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Source Code ‡¶è. Comment ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Source Code ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ HTML Comment Browser ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ Comment ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá Document ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Html Comment ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤:
    
    ```html
    <!-- Write your comments here -->  ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Html Comment Block. ‡¶è‡¶á Block ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Comment ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Code Hide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø Browser ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡ß®,‡ß© ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï Line Comment ‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    
    <p>This is a paragraph.</p>
    <!--
    <p>Look at this cool image:</p>
    <img border="0" src="pic_trulli.jpg" alt="Trulli">
    -->
    <p>This is a paragraph too.</p>
    ```
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶®  ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á , Html Link ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?
    
    HTML Document ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Web Page ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Link ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá HTML Link ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ HTML Link ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Hyperlinks ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Hyperlinks ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Link ‡¶è Click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá Jump ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Current Web Page ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Another Web Page ‡¶è ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Document ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element Hyperlink ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶á element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ Mouse Cursor ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá Cursor ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Little Hand`(üëÜüèø)` ‡¶è change ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Hyperlink. Example:
    
    ```html
    <a href="url">link text</a>  
    <a> ‡¶è‡¶á Tag ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Anchor Tag ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Element ‡¶ï‡ßá Link ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ 
    ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **href** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Link ‡¶è‡¶∞ Destination ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ Example:
    <a href="https://www.example.com/">Visit example.com</a>
    ```
    
    HTML Link ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ Text ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Element ‡¶ï‡ßá Hyperlink ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Image File ‡¶ï‡ßá Hyperlink ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ Example ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡•§
    
    ```html
    <a href="https://www.example.com">
       <img src="./flower.png" alt="Flower Image" style="width:42px; height:42px;">
    </a>
    ```
    
    HTML Link ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ Link, Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Tab ‡¶è Open ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á Tab ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø, ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Tab ‡¶è Open ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø **`target`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡•§ 
    
    Most Useful **`target`** Attribute Value are:
    
    - **`_self`**  ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ By Default ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Document ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á Tab ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶ì‡¶á Tab ‡¶è‡¶á Open ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    - **`_blank`** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ Document ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Tab Open ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Tab ‡¶è Open ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    
    ```html
    <a href="https://www.example.com/" target="_blank">Visit here!</a>
    ```
    
    **Absolute URLs vs. Relative URLs**
    
    - Absolute URL(A Full Web Address)
    - Relatives URL(https://www Part ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ Same Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Page)
    
    ```html
    <h2>Absolute URLs</h2>
    <p><a href="https://www.facebook.com/">Facebook</a></p>
    <p><a href="https://www.google.com/">Google</a></p>
    
    <h2>Relative URLs</h2>
    <p><a href="home.asp">Home Page</a></p>
    <p><a href="./css/default.asp">CSS Tutorial</a></p>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`href`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **`mailto:`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá User ‡¶è‡¶∞ Email Program ‡¶ñ‡ßã‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Link ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <a href="mailto:someone@example.com">Send email</a>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`title`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Element ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Specific Extra Information ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Information ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® Mouse Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ Hover ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® Tooltip Text ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá Show ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <a href="https://www.example.com" title="Go to example cite"> Visit </a>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`download`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Link ‡¶ï‡ßá Downloadable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá User ‡¶ï‡ßá Website ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Document Download ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <a href="./flower.png" download >Download Here</a>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>***Create a Bookmark in HTML***</ins>
    
    Bookmark ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßú‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Web Page ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶≤‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Bookmark ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá - ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá Bookmark ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ Link ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® User Link ‡¶è Click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® Web Page ‡¶ü‡¶ø Jump ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Bookmark ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßÄ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá Scroll ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Bookmark ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Always HTML Element ‡¶è **`id`** Attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<body>
    			<p><a href="#C4">Jump to Chapter 4</a></p>
    			<p><a href="#C10">Jump to Chapter 10</a></p>
    			<p><a href="#C17">Jump to Chapter 17</a></p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 1</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 2</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 3</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2 id="C4">Chapter 4</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 5</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 6</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 7</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 8</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 9</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2 id="C10">Chapter 10</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 11</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 12</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 13</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 14</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 15</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 16</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2 id="C17">Chapter 17</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 18</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 19</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 20</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 21</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 22</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    			
    			<h2>Chapter 23</h2>
    			<p>This chapter explains ba bla bla</p>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```

- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶®  ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á , Html Image, Picture Element ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?
    
    HTML Web Page ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`<img>`** Tag Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Image Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Image ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Design Improve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ **`<img>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Image ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ Image ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø **`<img>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá **`src`** Attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ **`<img>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Empty Tag. HTML Document ‡¶è Image ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ Syntax:
    
    ```html
    <img src="url" alt="alternatetext">
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`src`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá Image ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ Path ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ **`alt`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá  ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Alternative Text ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã Path ‡¶è Image ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á Text ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø **`<img>`** Tag ‡¶è ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶∂‡¶á **`alt`** Attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶ø Best Practices ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§   Example:
    
    ```html
    <img src="flower.jpg" alt="Flower">
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ **`height`**, **`width`** Attribute  ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ **`style`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Image ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßà‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ò‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ì ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <!-- with height and width Attribute -->
    <img src="flower.jpg" alt="Flower" width="500" height="600">
    <!-- with style Attribute -->
    <img src="flower.jpg" alt="Flower" style="width:500px;height:600px;">
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Folder ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Image ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Path ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Image ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‚Äù `/` ‚Äù ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Folder ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá **`src`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶õ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ images ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ï ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Folder ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Image ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É
    
    ```html
    <img src="/images/flower.jpg" alt="Flower">
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá Image Server ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Website ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶á Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ Image URL ‡¶ü‡¶æ **`src`** Attribute ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <img src="https://www.example.com/images/flower.jpg" alt="Flower">
    ```
    
    **`(Advance Topic)`** ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Website Browser ‡¶è Load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ Load ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá A to Z‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé Text, Images, Videos ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Webpage ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Load ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Network ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Bandwidth ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶ñ‡¶∞‡¶ö ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`loading`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`lazy`** Value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßü Website ‡¶è Image Load ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ Control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Network ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Bandwidth ‡¶ñ‡¶∞‡¶ö ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ **`loading`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`lazy`** Value ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤, Viewport**(**‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Device ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ü‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßÅ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü**)** ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶¶‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßå‡¶Å‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ Image Load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ó‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Scroll ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Image ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶ø Image ‡¶ü‡¶æ Load ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <img src="flower.jpg" alt="Flower" loading="lazy">
    ```
    
   
   > üí° <ins>***Note***</ins>: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Image ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Iframes Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§
    
    ### <ins>***Common Image Formats***</ins>
    
    ‡¶∏‡¶¨ Browser(Chrome, Edge, Firefox, Safari, Opera) ‡¶è Support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ Image File Types ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤:
    
    | Abbreviation | File Format | File Extension |
    | --- | --- | --- |
    | APNG | Animated Portable Network Graphics | .apng |
    | GIF | Graphics Interchange Format | .gif |
    | ICO | Microsoft Icon | .ico, .cur |
    | JPEG | Joint Photographic Expert Group image | .jpg, .jpeg, .jfif, .pjpeg, .pjp |
    | PNG | Portable Network Graphics | .png |
    | SVG | Scalable Vector Graphics | .svg |
    
    ### <ins>*HTML Picture Element:*</ins>
    
    HTML **`<picture>`** Element Web Developer ‡¶ï‡ßá Image Resource ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá Flexibility ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ **`<picture>`** Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï **`<source>`** Elements ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`<source>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **`srcset`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Images ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ Path/URL ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`media`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Device ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Device ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá Image ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Browser Choose ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<head>
    			<meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    	</head>
    	<body>
          <h2>The picture Element</h2>
    			<picture>
    			  <source media="(min-width: 650px)" srcset="https://images.pexels.com/photos/376464/pexels-photo-376464.jpeg?auto=compress&cs=tinysrgb&w=600">
    			  <source media="(min-width: 465px)" srcset="https://images.pexels.com/photos/1805053/pexels-photo-1805053.jpeg?auto=compress&cs=tinysrgb&w=600">
    			  <img src="https://images.pexels.com/photos/2565222/pexels-photo-2565222.jpeg?auto=compress&cs=tinysrgb&w=600" style="width:auto;">
    			</picture>
    			<p>Resize the browser to see different versions of the picture loading at different viewport sizes.
    			The browser looks for the first source element where the media query matches the user's current viewport width,
    			and fetches the image specified in the srcset attribute.</p>
    
    			<p>The img element is required as the last child tag of the picture declaration block.
    			The img element is used to provide backward compatibility for browsers that do not support the picture element, or if none of the source tags matched.
    			</p>
    			
    			<p><strong>Note:</strong> The picture element is not supported in IE12 and earlier or Safari 9.0 and earlier.</p>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    
    > üí° <ins>***Note***</ins> : ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü **`<picture>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Last Child ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **`<img/>`** Element ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Browser ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø **`<picture>`** Element Support ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ **`<source>`** Element Match ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá **`<img/>`** Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø Display ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ **`<img/>`** Element ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Browser Support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
  
    
    ‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ **`<picture>`** Element ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨:
    
    ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ Main Purposes ‡¶è **`<picture>`** Element ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤:
    
    1. <ins>**Bandwidth**</ins>  ‚áí ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Website ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü Screen Or Device ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Run ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßú Image File Load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§ Browser Device ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá **`<source>`** Element ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Image File ‡¶ü‡¶ø load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø Elements ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Ignore ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Bandwidth ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    2. <ins>**Format Support**</ins> ‚áí  ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Browser ‡¶¨‡¶æ Device ‡¶∏‡¶¨ Image Format Support ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`<picture>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ Image Format Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡•§ Browser ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá Format ‡¶ü‡¶ø Support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Ignore ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    
    Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<head>
    			<meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    	</head>
    	<body>
    			<h2>The picture Element</h2>
    			<picture>
    			  <source srcset="https://images.pexels.com/photos/5255232/pexels-photo-5255232.jpeg?auto=compress&cs=tinysrgb&w=600">
    			  <source srcset="https://images.pexels.com/photos/6833459/pexels-photo-6833459.jpeg?auto=compress&cs=tinysrgb&w=600">
    			  <img src="https://images.pexels.com/photos/6177639/pexels-photo-6177639.jpeg?auto=compress&cs=tinysrgb&w=600" alt="Desk" style="width:auto;">
    			</picture>
    			<p>The picture element can be used when the image format is not supported by all devices.</p>
    			<p>The device will use the first image format it supports, and ignore the rest of the images.</p>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
 
  >  üí° <ins>***Note***</ins>: Browser Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ **`<source>`** Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø Element ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Ignore ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

    
    ### <ins>***HTML Figure and Figcaption  Element***</ins>
    
    Html **`<figure>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Image ‡¶ï‡ßá Mark ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá **`<figcaption>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ  ‡¶ê Image ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Caption ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<body>
    		<h1>The figure and figcaption element</h1>
    		<figure>
    		  <img src="flower.jpg" alt="Flower" style="width:100%">
    		  <figcaption>Fig.1 - Flower image.</figcaption>
    		</figure>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ***[Learn HTML \<map> and \<area> Elements Here.](https://www.w3schools.com/html/html_images_imagemap.asp)***
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶®  ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á , Html Video Element ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?
    
    HTML Document ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`<video>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Video Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ HTML5 ‡¶è Video Tag Support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <video width="500" height="300" controls>
       <source src="./Gordon Goose_ Weekend! _ Funny animated short film.mp4" type="video/mp4">
       <source src="./Gordon Goose_ Weekend! _ Funny animated short film.webm" type="video/webM">
        Your browser does not support the video tag.
    </video>
    ```
    
    Image Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ Video Tag, Video Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá Help ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Video ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ **`src`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Video ‡¶è‡¶∞ Path ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ 
    
    - ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`height`** and **`width`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Video ‡¶è‡¶∞ Height ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Width Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    - ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`controls`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Video Control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Video Play, Push ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Volume Control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§
    - ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`<source>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá  Alternative Video File ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á Browser ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á File Format Support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Browser ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á File ‡¶ü‡¶æ  Choose ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶æ Support ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ Text ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá HTML Video Tag ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Video Formats Support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ There are: $mp4, webm, ogg.$
    
    ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Browser ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø File Formats Support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤:
   
    | Browser Name | mp4 | webM |ogg |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | Internet Explorer | Yes | No | No |
    | Google Chrome | Yes | Yes | Yes |
    | Mozilla Firefox|Yes|Yes|Yes|
    | Opera|Yes|Yes|Yes|
    | Safari|Yes|No|No|

    > üí° <ins>**Note**</ins>: Android ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ mp4 file support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`autoplay`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Video Automatically Start ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® Browser Load ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶®, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`loop`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Video ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ **`muted`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Video Sound Mute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <video width="500" height="300" controls autoplay muted loop>
       <source src="./Gordon Goose_ Weekend! _ Funny animated short film.mp4" type="video/mp4">
       <source src="./Gordon Goose_ Weekend! _ Funny animated short film.webm" type="video/webM">
        Your browser does not support the video tag.
    </video>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`poster`** Attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Video ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ Thumbnail ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ 
    
    ```html
    <video width="500" height="300" controls poster="./Gooldren_Duck_Poster.jpg">
       <source src="./Gordon Goose_ Weekend! _ Funny animated short film.mp4" type="video/mp4">
       <source src="./Gordon Goose_ Weekend! _ Funny animated short film.webm" type="video/webM">
        Your browser does not support the video tag.
    </video>
    ```
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶®  ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á , Html Audio Element ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?
    
    HTML Document ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`<audio>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Audio Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ HTML5 Audio Tag Support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <audio controls>
      <source src="./small-river-in-the-forest-very-close-sound-effect.mp3" type="audio/mp3">
      <source src="./small-river-in-the-forest-very-close-sound-effect.wav" type="audio/wav">
       Your browser does not support the audio element.
    </audio>
    ```
    
    HTML **`<video>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ **`<audio>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Web Page ‡¶è Audio File Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì **`controls`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Audio Control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Audio Play, Push ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Volume Control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ 
    
    ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`<source>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá  Alternative Audio File ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Browser ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á File Format Support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ Choose ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶æ Support ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ Text ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá HTML **`<audio>`** Tag ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ Audio Formats Support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ There are: $mp3, wev, ogg.$
    
    ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Browser ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø File Formats Support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤:
    
  | Browser Name|mp3|wav|ogg|
  | --- | --- | --- | --- |
  | Internet Explorer|Yes|No|No|
  | Google Chrome|Yes|Yes|Yes|
  | Mozilla Firefox|Yes|Yes|Yes|
  | Opera|No|Yes|Yes |
  | Safari|Yes|Yes|No |
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`autoplay`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Audio Automatically Start ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`loop`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Audio ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ **`muted`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Audio Sound Mute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <audio controls autoplay muted loop>
      <source src="./small-river-in-the-forest-very-close-sound-effect.mp3" type="audio/mp3">
      <source src="./small-river-in-the-forest-very-close-sound-effect.wav" type="audio/wav">
       Your browser does not support the audio element.
    </audio>
    ```
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶®  ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á , Html List Element ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?
    
    HTML List ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Information List ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ List ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï  List Element ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§  
    
    Html ‡¶è ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ List ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤ :
    
    - Ordered List or Numbered List (ol)
    - Unordered List or Bulleted List (ul)
    - Description List or Definition List (dl)
    
    ### <ins>Ordered HTML List</ins> :
    
    HTML **`<ol>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Browser ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Ordered List. ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Ordered List Numerical or Alphabetical ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Ordered List Start ‡¶π‡ßü **`<ol>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø List ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü **`<li>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <ol>
      <li> Apple </li>
      <li> Mango </li>
      <li> Banana </li>
    </ol>
    ```
    
    HTML Ordered List By Default Numeric Value ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`type`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Value ‡¶ü‡¶æ Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    
    ```html
    Numbers:
    <ol type="1">
      <li>Coffee</li>
      <li>Tea</li>
      <li>Milk</li>
    </ol>
    
    Uppercase Letters:
    <ol type="A">
      <li>Coffee</li>
      <li>Tea</li>
      <li>Milk</li>
    </ol>
    
    Lowercase Letters:
    <ol type="a">
      <li>Coffee</li>
      <li>Tea</li>
      <li>Milk</li>
    </ol>
    
    Uppercase Roman Numbers:
    <ol type="I">
      <li>Coffee</li>
      <li>Tea</li>
      <li>Milk</li>
    </ol>
    
    Lowercase Roman Numbers:
    <ol type="i">
      <li>Coffee</li>
      <li>Tea</li>
      <li>Milk</li>
    </ol>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá List Counting Control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø By Default Ordered List Count Start ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá 1 ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`start`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Specified ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Number ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <ol start="50">
      <li>Apple</li>
      <li>Mango</li>
      <li>Banana</li>
    </ol>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ List ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ List ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Nested List ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <ol>
      <li>Coffee</li>
      <li>Tea
        <ol>
          <li>Black tea</li>
          <li>Green tea</li>
        </ol>
      </li>
      <li>Milk</li>
    </ol>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>Unordered HTML List</ins> :
    
    HTML **`<ul>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Browser ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Unordered list. Unordered List Start ‡¶π‡ßü **`<ul>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø List ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü **`<li>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <ul>
      <li>Mango</li>
      <li>Apple</li>
      <li>Banana</li>
    </ul>
    ```
    
    HTML Unordered List By Default Bullets(small black circles) Marked ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`type`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Marked ‡¶ü‡¶æ Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!-- Example - Disc -->
    <ul type='disc'>
      <li>Coffee</li>
      <li>Tea</li>
      <li>Milk</li>
    </ul>
    
    <!-- Example - Circle -->
    <ul type="circle">
      <li>Coffee</li>
      <li>Tea</li>
      <li>Milk</li>
    </ul>
    
    <!-- Example - Square -->
    <ul type="square">
      <li>Coffee</li>
      <li>Tea</li>
      <li>Milk</li>
    </ul>
    
    <!-- Example - None -->
    <ul type="none">
      <li>Coffee</li>
      <li>Tea</li>
      <li>Milk</li>
    </ul>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>HTML Description List</ins> :
    
    HTML ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø description List ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ List ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá List Item ‡¶è‡¶∞ Definition ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ HTML Description List ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Information ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Example :
    
    ```html
    <dl>
      <dt>‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ç</dt>
      <dd>‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶ü‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡•§</dd>
      
      <dt>‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü</dt>
      <dd>‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶®‡ßã‡¶≤‡¶ú‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§</dd>
      
      <dt>‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ü (CSS)</dt>
      <dd>‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÉ‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ‡•§</dd>
    </dl>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`<dl>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Browser ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Description List. ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ **`<dt>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ List ‡¶è‡¶∞ Title ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`<dd>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ì‡¶á Title ‡¶è‡¶∞ Description ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶®  ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á , Html Table Element ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ HTML **`<table>`** Tag Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Web Page ‡¶è Data ‡¶ï‡ßá Tabular Form (row * column) ‡¶è Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Row ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Columns ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <table border='1'>
    <caption> My Table Name </caption>
      <tr>
        <th>Name</th>
        <th>Class</th>
        <th>Roll</th>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td>Habib</td>
        <td>One</td>
        <td>01</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td>Karim</td>
        <td>One</td>
        <td>02</td>
      </tr>
    </table>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`<table>`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **`border`** Attribute Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Table ‡¶è‡¶∞ Border ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ 
    
    - **`<caption>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Table ‡¶è‡¶∞ Caption ‡¶¨‡¶æ Table Name ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    - ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`<tr>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Table ‡¶è‡¶∞ Row ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Table ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶§  Row ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶á Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡•§
    - **`<th>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Table ‡¶è‡¶∞ Heading ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø Table ‡¶è Heading ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Table Data. ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ü‡¶æ Heading Element ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ Table ‡¶è ‡¶§‡¶§‡¶ü‡¶æ Column ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    - **`<td>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Table Data ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø **`<td>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Column ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`style`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Table ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <table border='1' style="width:50%">
    <caption> My Table Name </caption>
      <tr>
        <th>Name</th>
        <th>Class</th>
        <th>Roll</th>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td>Habib</td>
        <td>One</td>
        <td>01</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td>Karim</td>
        <td>One</td>
        <td>02</td>
      </tr>
    </table>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ Table ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Column ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Column ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`colspan`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ **`colspan`** Attribute **`<th>`** Or **`<td>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ **`colspan`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßü‡¶ü‡¶æ Column ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Column ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Number ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Multiple Row ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Column ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø **`rowspan`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Attribute ‡¶ì **`<th>`** Or **`<td>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßü‡¶ü‡¶æ Row ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Column ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Number ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <table border='1' style="width:50%">
    <caption> My Table Name </caption>
      <tr>
        <th colspan='2'> Name</th>
        <th rowspan='2'>Class</th>
        <th rowspan='2'>Roll</th>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <th>First Name</th>
        <th>Last Name</th>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td>Jabedul</td>
        <td>Islam</td>
        <td>One</td>
        <td>01</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td>Aminul</td>
        <td>Islam</td>
        <td>One</td>
        <td>02</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td>Habibur</td>
        <td>Rahaman</td>
        <td>One</td>
        <td>03</td>
      </tr>
    </table>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Table ‡¶ï‡ßá Head, Body, Footer ‡¶è ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Table ‡¶ï‡ßá Control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Easy ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ **`<thead>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Group Of Header Content ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ **`<tbody>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Group Of Body Content ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ **`<tfoot>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Group Of Footer Content ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <table border='1' style='width: 50%'>
      <thead>
        <tr>
          <th>Month</th>
          <th>Savings</th>
        </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
        <tr>
          <td>January</td>
          <td>$100</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td>February</td>
          <td>$80</td>
        </tr>
      </tbody>
      <tfoot>
        <tr>
          <td>Sum</td>
          <td>$180</td>
        </tr>
      </tfoot>
    </table>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Development ‡¶è Table ‡¶ï‡ßá Part By Part Control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Head ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ Style ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨, Body ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ Style ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨, Footer ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ Style ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <table border='1' style='width:50%'>
      <thead style="color: green">
        <tr>
          <th>Month</th>
          <th>Savings</th>
        </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody style="color: blue">
        <tr>
          <td>January</td>
          <td>$100</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td>February</td>
          <td>$80</td>
        </tr>
      </tbody>
      <tfoot style="color: orange">
        <tr>
          <td>Sum</td>
          <td>$180</td>
        </tr>
      </tfoot>
    </table>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>Table Colgroup Element</ins> :
    
    HTML **`<colgroup>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Table ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Columns Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø Group ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **`<col>`** Element ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`span`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßü‡¶ü‡¶ø Column ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ **`style`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Column ‡¶è‡¶∞ Style ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ **`<colgroup>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá CSS Properties ‡¶è‡¶∞ limited Selector ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ **`width`** Property, **`visibility`** Property, **`background`** Property, **`border`** Property. ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø CSS Property ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá Table ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Effect ‡¶™‡ßú‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ Example :
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<body>
    			<h2>Colgroup Element</h2>
    			<table border="1" style="width: 50%;">
    				<caption> My Calander </caption>
    				<colgroup>
    				  <col span="4">
    				  <col span="1" style ="background-color: #ff3322;width:150px;">
    				</colgroup>
    				<tr>
    					<th>MON</th>
    					<th>TUE</th>
    					<th>WED</th>
    					<th>THU</th>
    					<th>FRI</th>
    					<th>SAT</th>
    					<th>SUN</th>
    				</tr>
    				<tr>
    					<td>1</td>
    					<td>2</td>
    					<td>3</td>
    					<td>4</td>
    					<td>5</td>
    					<td>6</td>
    					<td>7</td>
    				</tr>
    				<tr>
    					<td>8</td>
    					<td>9</td>
    					<td>10</td>
    					<td>11</td>
    					<td>12</td>
    					<td>13</td>
    					<td>14</td>
    				</tr>
    				<tr>
    					<td>15</td>
    					<td>16</td>
    					<td>17</td>
    					<td>18</td>
    					<td>19</td>
    					<td>20</td>
    					<td>21</td>
    				</tr>
    				<tr>
    					<td>22</td>
    					<td>23</td>
    					<td>24</td>
    					<td>25</td>
    					<td>26</td>
    					<td>27</td>
    					<td>28</td>
    				</tr>
    			</table>
    			<br>
    			<h2>Add Visibility Property </h2>
    			<table border="1" style="width: 50%;">
    				<caption> My Calander </caption>
    				<colgroup>
    				  <col span="4">
    				  <col span="1" style ="background-color: #ff3322; visibility:collapse;">
    				</colgroup>
    				<tr>
    					<th>MON</th>
    					<th>TUE</th>
    					<th>WED</th>
    					<th>THU</th>
    					<th>FRI</th>
    					<th>SAT</th>
    					<th>SUN</th>
    				</tr>
    				<tr>
    					<td>1</td>
    					<td>2</td>
    					<td>3</td>
    					<td>4</td>
    					<td>5</td>
    					<td>6</td>
    					<td>7</td>
    				</tr>
    				<tr>
    					<td>8</td>
    					<td>9</td>
    					<td>10</td>
    					<td>11</td>
    					<td>12</td>
    					<td>13</td>
    					<td>14</td>
    				</tr>
    				<tr>
    					<td>15</td>
    					<td>16</td>
    					<td>17</td>
    					<td>18</td>
    					<td>19</td>
    					<td>20</td>
    					<td>21</td>
    				</tr>
    				<tr>
    					<td>22</td>
    					<td>23</td>
    					<td>24</td>
    					<td>25</td>
    					<td>26</td>
    					<td>27</td>
    					<td>28</td>
    				</tr>
    			</table>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
   
   > üí° <ins>***Note***</ins> : **`<colgroup>`** Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **`<table>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Child Element ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® **`<table>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® **`<thead>`**, **`<tr>`**, **`<td>`** ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá **`<caption>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
