- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶®  ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á ,  Html Iframes Element ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?
    
    ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Webpage Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá Iframe Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ HTML **`<iframe>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <iframe src="url" title="description"></iframe>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`src`** Attribute ‡¶è Resource URL ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`title`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Title ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá Good Practice ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Title ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Iframe ‡¶è‡¶∞ Content ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ 
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Iframe ‡¶è‡¶∞ Height ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Width ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨ **`style`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <iframe src="./demo.html" style="height:300px;width:600px" title="Iframe Example"></iframe>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Link ‡¶ï‡ßá Target ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Iframe ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Open ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <iframe name="iframe_b" height="400px"width="100%" title="Iframe Example"></iframe>
    <p> <a href="https://www.wikipedia.org/" target="iframe_b"> Go to Wikipadia</a></p>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`<iframe>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá YouTube Video Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá YouTube Video Id ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ **`<iframe>`**Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`src`** Attribute ‡¶è URL Path ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‚Äú**`https://youtube.com/embed`**‚Äù ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‚Äú**`/`**‚Äù ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá YouTube Video ID ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <iframe width="50%" height="350" src="https://youtube.com/embed/l78u3rdxoVU" title="ChatGPT ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ü ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶°‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®">
    </iframe>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ YouTube Video Full Screen Mode **ON** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`allowfullscreen`** Attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Source URL ‡¶è **`autoplay=1`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá video Automatically Play ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`mute=1`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Video Sound Mute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`loop=1`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Video Looping ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá Video Looping ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á **`playlist=VideoID`** Parameter ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example :
    
    ```html
    <iframe width="50%" height="350" src="https://youtube.com/embed/l78u3rdxoVU?mute=1&autoplay=1" title="ChatGPT ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ü ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶°‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®" allowfullscreen></iframe>
    
    <iframe width="50%" height="350" src="https://youtube.com/embed/l78u3rdxoVU?playlist=l78u3rdxoVU&loop=1" title="ChatGPT ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ü ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶°‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®"  allowfullscreen></iframe>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`controls=0`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá YouTube Video ‡¶è‡¶∞ Player Controls Display ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá User ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ Control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ By Default Player Controls Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`controls=1`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ì Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example :
    
    ```html
    <iframe width="420" height="315" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/tgbNymZ7vqY?controls=0"></iframe>
    ```
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶®  ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á , Html From Element ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?
    
    HTML **`<form>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ User Input ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ Form ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form>
    .
    form elements
    .
    </form>
    ```
    
    **`<from>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Input ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ Different Input Type ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Text Field, Checkboxes, Radio Buttons, Buttons, Submit Buttons ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ HTML **`<input>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Input Field ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`type`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Input Type ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ 
    
    ### <ins>***Text Fields:***</ins>
    
    **`<input type="text">`**¬† ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Single-Line Input ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form>
      <label for="fname">First name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="fname" name="fname" placeholder="enter your firstname"><br>
      <label for="lname">Last name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="lname" name="lname" placeholder="enter your lastname"><br>
    </form>
    ```
    
    - ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`<label>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Input Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Label ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ **`<label>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **`for`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨ Label ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Input Field ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    - **`<input>`** Element ‡¶è **`type`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Input Type ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ **`id`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Input Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Unique ID ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, **`name`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Input Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Name ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ User Input Data ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ **`placeholder`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Hints ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø User ‡¶ï‡ßá, Input Field ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶ø Input ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡•§ **`placeholder`** Attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü (text, search, url, tel, email, and password) Input Field ‡¶è‡•§
    - ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`<br>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Line Break ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
    
    **`disabled`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Input Field ‡¶ï‡ßá Disable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <form>
      <label for="fname">First name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="fname" name="fname" placeholder="enter your firstname" disabled><br>
      <label for="lname">Last name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="lname" name="lname" placeholder="enter your lastname"><br>
    </form>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`maxLength`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Input Field ‡¶è‡¶∞ Number Of Character ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form>
      <label for="fname">First name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="fname" name="fname" placeholder="enter your firstname" maxLength="5"><br>
      <label for="lname">Last name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="lname" name="lname" placeholder="enter your lastname"><br>
    </form>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`readonly`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Field ‡¶è‡¶∞ Data ‡¶ï‡ßá Non-Editable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Input Field ‡¶è **`value`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Default ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Value Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example :
    
    ```html
    <form>
      <label for="fname">First name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="fname" name="fname" value="Shahidul" readonly><br>
      <label for="lname">Last name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="lname" name="lname"><br>
    </form>
    ```
    
    **`size`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Text Field ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ **`size`** Attribute ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Input Field ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤:- text, search, tel, url, email, and password. Example :
    
    ```html
    <form>
      <label for="fname">First name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="fname" name="fname" value="Shahidul" readonly><br>
      <label for="lname">Last name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="lname" name="lname" size="30"><br>
    </form>
    ```
    
    **`required`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Input Field ‡¶ï‡ßá Must Be Filled ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ Functionality Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ User Required Field Fill ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Form Submit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ **`required`** Attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá (text, search, url, tel, email, password, date pickers, number, checkbox, radio, and file) Input Field ‡¶è‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form action="#">
      <label for="fname">First name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="fname" name="fname" placeholder="enter your firstname" required><br>
      <label for="lname">Last name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="lname" name="lname" placeholder="enter your lastname"><br><br>
      <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    </form>
    ```
    
    **`autofocus`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Input Field ‡¶ï‡ßá Automatically Focus ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® Page Load ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form>
      <label for="fname">First name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="fname" name="fname" autofocus><br>
      <label for="lname">Last name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="lname" name="lname">
    </form>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>*Password Fields*</ins> :
    
    **`<input type="password">`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Password Field ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Password Field ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Input Text ‡¶ï‡ßá User ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Invisible ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ Password Field User ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Password ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form>
      <label for="username">Username:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="username" name="username"><br>
      <label for="pwd">Password:</label><br>
      <input type="password" id="pwd" name="pwd">
    </form>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>*Email Fields*</ins> :
    
    **`<input type="email">`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Email Address ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Validate Email Address Input ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form action="#">
      <label for="email">Enter your email:</label>
      <input type="email" id="email" name="email">
      <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    </form>
    ```
    
    Email Input Field ‡¶è **`multiple`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Multiple Email Input ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø User ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <form action="#">
      <label for="email">Enter your email:</label>
      <input type="email" id="email" name="email" multiple>
      <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    </form>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>*Radio Buttons*</ins> :
    
    **`<input type="radio">`**¬†Defines a Radio Button. Radio Button ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Number ‡¶¨‡¶æ Data Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá **`name`** Attribute ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Value Same ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form>
      <label>Gender:</label>
    ¬† <input type="radio" id="male" name="gender" value="male">
    ¬† <label for="male">Male</label>
    ¬† <input type="radio" id="female" name="gender" value="female">
    ¬† <label for="female">Female</label><br>
    </form>
    ```
    
    **`checked`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Radio Button ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Value ‡¶ï‡ßá By Default Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <form>
      <label>Gender:</label>
    ¬† <input type="radio" id="male" name="gender" value="male" checked>
    ¬† <label for="male">Male</label>
    ¬† <input type="radio" id="female" name="gender" value="female">
    ¬† <label for="female">Female</label><br>
    </form>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>*Checkboxes*</ins> :
    
    **`<input type="checkbox">`**¬†Defines a¬†Checkbox. Checkbox ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Multiple Number Of Data Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example
    
    ```html
    <form>
      <label>Select your favourite Subjects </label><br>
      <input type="checkbox" id="bangla" name="subject1" value="bangla">
      <label for="bangla">Bangla</label><br>
      <input type="checkbox" id="english" name="subject2" value="english">
      <label for="english">English</label><br>
      <input type="checkbox" id="math" name="subject3" value="math">
      <label for="math">Math</label>
    </form>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>*Dropdownlist*</ins> :
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ HTML **`<select>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Dropdown List ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form >
      <label for="colors">Choose a color:</label>
      <select id="colors" name="colors">
        <option value="red">Red</option>
        <option value="blue">Blue</option>
        <option value="green">Green</option>
        <option value="black">Black</option>
        <option value="white">White</option>
      </select>
    </form>
    
    <!--with selected Attribute -->
    <form >
      <label for="colors">Choose a color:</label>
      <select id="colors" name="colors">
        <option value="red">Red</option>
        <option value="blue" selected>Blue</option>
        <option value="green">Green</option>
        <option value="black">Black</option>
        <option value="white">White</option>
      </select>
    </form>
    ```
    
    - ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`<option>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá **`<select>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® Option Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    - **`<option>`** Element ‡¶è **`value`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Option ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`selected`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Value ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`size`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßü‡¶ü‡¶æ value dropdown ‡¶è show ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form >
      <label for="colors">Choose a color:</label>
      <select id="colors" name="colors" size='3'>
        <option value="red">Red</option>
        <option value="blue">Blue</option>
        <option value="green">Green</option>
        <option value="black">Black</option>
        <option value="white">White</option>
      </select>
    </form>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`multiple`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Dropdown ‡¶è Multiple Value Select Allow ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá Keyboard ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`Ctrl Button`** ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form>
      <label for="colors">Choose a color:</label>
      <select id="colors" name="colors" size='3' multiple>
        <option value="red">Red</option>
        <option value="blue">Blue</option>
        <option value="green">Green</option>
        <option value="black">Black</option>
        <option value="white">White</option>
      </select>
    </form>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`<optgroup>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Dropdown List ‡¶è‡¶∞ Option ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Group ‡¶è ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form>
      <label for="cars">Choose a car:</label>
      <select name="cars" id="cars">
        <optgroup label="Swedish Cars" disabled>
          <option value="volvo">Volvo</option>
          <option value="saab">Saab</option>
        </optgroup>
        <optgroup label="German Cars">
          <option value="mercedes">Mercedes</option>
          <option value="audi">Audi</option>
        </optgroup>
      </select>
    </form>
    ```
    
    - **`<optgroup>`** Element ‡¶è **`label`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Group Name ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`disabled`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶á Group ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Disable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    
    ### <ins>*TextArea Element*</ins> :
    
    **`<textarea>`** Element ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Multi-Line Input Field ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Multi-Line Input, User ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form >
      <label for="message">Message</label><br>
      <textarea name="message" rows="10" cols="40"> </textarea>
    </form>
    ```
    
    - ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`row`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`<textarea>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶§‡¶ü‡¶æ Line Visible ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ **`col`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá  **`<textarea>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width ‡¶ï‡¶§‡¶ü‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßÅ Visible ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    
    ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`style`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá **`<textarea>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Height ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Width ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example :
    
    ```html
    <form >
      <label for="message">Message</label><br>
      <textarea name="message" style="width:300px; height:300px;"> </textarea>
    </form>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>*Data-List Element*</ins> :
    
    **`<datalist>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Input Fields ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Data Pre-Defined ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form>
      <input list="browsers" name="browser">
      <datalist id="browsers">
        <option value="Internet Explorer">
        <option value="Firefox">
        <option value="Chrome">
        <option value="Opera">
        <option value="Safari">
      </datalist>
    </form>
    ```
    
    - ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`list`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Input Field ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® **`<datalist>`** Element ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ Id ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ **`<datalist>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`id`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Unique ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Id ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá **`<datalist>`** Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø Access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ **`<option>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`value`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`<datalist>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
    
    ### <ins>*Fieldset & Legend*</ins> :
    
    **`<fieldset>`** Element ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Form ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Related Data ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Group ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ **`<legend>`** Element ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Group ‡¶è‡¶∞ Caption Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<body>
    			<h2>Grouping Form Data with Fieldset</h2>
    			<p>The fieldset element is used to group related data in a form, and the legend element defines a caption for the fieldset element.</p>
    			<form action="#">
    			  <fieldset>
    			    <legend>Personal:</legend>
    			    <label for="fname">First name:</label><br>
    			    <input type="text" id="fname" name="fname" value="Shahidul"><br>
    			    <label for="lname">Last name:</label><br>
    			    <input type="text" id="lname" name="lname" value="Islam"><br><br>
    			    <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    			  </fieldset>
    			</form>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>*File Input Fields*</ins> :
    
    **`<input type="file">`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Computer Directory  ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® File Browse ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Upload ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Submit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <form action="#">
      <label for="myfile">Select a file:</label>
      <input type="file" id="myfile" name="myfile"><br><br>
      <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    </form>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`multiple`** Attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Multiple Image Select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form action="#">
      <label for="myfile">Select Multiple files:</label>
      <input type="file" id="myfile" name="myfile" multiple><br><br>
      <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    </form>
    ```
    
    ### *Hidden Input Fields:*
    
    **`<input type="hidden">`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Input Field ‡¶ï‡ßá User ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Hidden ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Hidden Field ‡¶è Data User ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá From Submit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá Hidden Field ‡¶è‡¶∞ Data Server ‡¶è Sent ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form action="#">
      <label for="fname">First name:</label>
      <input type="text" id="fname" name="fname">
      <input type="hidden" id="custId" name="custId" value="3487"><br><br>
     <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    </form>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>*Number Input Fields*</ins> :
    
    **`<input type="number">`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Number Input Field ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form action="#">
      <label for="quantity">Quantity</label>
      <input type="number" id="quantity" name="quantity">
      <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    </form>
    ```
    
    **`min`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`max`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Number Value ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ **`min`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`max`** Attribute ‡¶Ø‡ßá Input Field ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤:-  number, range, date, datetime-local, month, time and week. Example: 
    
    ```html
    <form action="#">
      <label for="quantity">Quantity (between 1 and 5):</label>
      <input type="number" id="quantity" name="quantity" min="1" max="5">
      <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    </form>
    ```
    
    Number Field ‡¶è **`step`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Number Value ‡¶ï‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ **`step`** Attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá (number, range, date, datetime-local, month, time and week) input field ‡¶è‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form action="#">
      <label for="quantity">Quantity:</label>
      <input type="number" id="quantity" name="quantity" min="0" max="100" step="10">
      <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    </form>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>*Button*</ins>:
    
    **`<button>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ clickable button ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <button type="button">Click Me!</button>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>*The Submit Button*</ins> :
    
    **`<input type="submit">`**¬†‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Web Page ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Submit Button ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® User Submit Button ‡¶è Click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® Form Data ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Form-Handler ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Server ‡¶è ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Form-Handler ‡¶π‡¶≤ Server Side ‡¶è‡¶∞ Code ‡¶¨‡¶æ Script, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Form Data ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Process ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ Result ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Form-Handler ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ Server ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® PHP, Python, Node.js, ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§ Form-Handler ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨ ‡¶π‡¶≤ Form ‡¶è ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ Data ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá Optional Validation, Database ‡¶è ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£, ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ø‡¶ï API Service ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Data ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶£, Mail ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã, File Upload ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶™ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡•§ Form-Handler Data ‡¶ï‡ßá Processing ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞, ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º Result ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ø‡¶æ User ‡¶ï‡ßá Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶™‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Redirect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form action="#">
      <label for="fname">First name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="fname" name="fname" placeholder="enter your firstname"><br>
      <label for="lname">Last name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="lname" name="lname" placeholder="enter your lastname"><br>
      <label>Gender:</label>
    ¬† <input type="radio" id="male" name="gender" value="male">
    ¬† <label for="male">Male</label>
    ¬† <input type="radio" id="female" name="gender" value="female">
    ¬† <label for="female">Female</label><br>
      <label>Select your favourite Subjects </label><br>
      <input type="checkbox" id="bangla" name="subject1" value="bangla">
      <label for="bangla">Bangla</label><br>
      <input type="checkbox" id="english" name="subject2" value="english">
      <label for="english">English</label><br>
      <input type="checkbox" id="math" name="subject3" value="math">
      <label for="math">Math</label><br>
      <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    </form>
    ```
    
    - **`action`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Form-Handler ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Form Data Server ‡¶è Sending ‡¶ì Processing ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ **`action`** Attribute ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ From Data Server ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡ßá Location ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
    
   
   > üí° <ins>***Note***</ins> : ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø Input Field ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ **`name`** Attribute ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá, Input Field ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Value ‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`target`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Server Response ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßü Display ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§  
    
    ¬†**`target`**¬†Attribute ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡ßá Value ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤:
    
    - **_blank** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Response ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Window ‡¶¨‡¶æ Tab ‡¶è Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    - **_self** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Response ‡¶ï‡ßá Current Window ‡¶§‡ßá Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    - **_parent** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Response ‡¶ï‡ßá Parent Frame ‡¶è Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    - **_top** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Response ‡¶ï‡ßá Window ‡¶è‡¶∞ Full Body ‡¶§‡ßá Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    - **framename** ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Response ‡¶ï‡ßá Name ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Iframe ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    
    Example :
    
    ```html
    <form action="#" target="_blank">
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`method`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá HTTP Method(get, post) ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨ Form Data Submit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü‡•§ Form Data ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Sent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ URL Variable(with **get** method) ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ HTTP Post Transaction(with **post** method). POST Method ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Encrypt Data Server ‡¶è Send ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ POST Method Submitted Data ‡¶ï‡ßá Encoded ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Server ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Data Secure ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ By Default Get Method ‡¶è Data Submit ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form action="#" method="get">
    ```
    
    <ins>***GET Method ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø***</ins> : 
    
    - Get Method From Data ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Name/Value ‡¶ú‡ßã‡ßú‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá URL ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
    - Sensitive Data Send ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá Get Method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ Get Method ‡¶è Data Submit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü From Data URL ‡¶è Visible ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    - Get Method ‡¶è URL Length Limited ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§(2048 Characters)
    - From Submissions ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá Get Method ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶á Useful ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ú‡¶® User, Submissions Result ‡¶ü‡¶ø  Bookmark ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá Save ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
    - Get Method, Non-Secure Data ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Google ‡¶è‡¶∞ Query String ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
    
    <ins>***POST Method ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø***</ins> :
    
    - Post Method ‡¶è From Data HTTP Request ‡¶è‡¶∞ Body ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá URL ‡¶è Data Show ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
    - POST Method ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Size Limitations ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ö‡ßÅ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® Data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
    - Post ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Data Submit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ Bookmark ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
    
    
   > üí° </ins>***Note***</ins> : Personal Information ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Sensitive Data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü  POST Method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§
  
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`autocomplete`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá User ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Extra Functionality ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Autocomplete On ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá User ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Type ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ Auto Show ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ User ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Type ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ Value ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Data Input Field ‡¶è Input ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Autocomplete Off ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ Type ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ Value Show ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Type ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ **`autocomplete`** Attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü(text, search, url, tel, email, password, datepickers, range, and color) Input Field ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form action="#" autocomplete="on">
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`novalidate`** Attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Validate ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ Data Server ‡¶è Sent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form action="#" novalidate>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>Reset Button</ins> :
    
    **`<input type="reset">`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Rest Button ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Reset Button Form ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ Input Value ‡¶ï‡ßá Default Value ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form action="#">
      <label for="fname">First name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="fname" name="fname"><br>
      <label for="lname">Last name:</label><br>
      <input type="text" id="lname" name="lname"><br><br>
      <input type="submit" value="Submit">
      <input type="reset">
    </form>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>***Tel input field***</ins> :
    
    **`<input type="tel">`**  ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Telephone ‡¶¨‡¶æ Mobile Phone Number Input ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form action="#">
      <label for="phone">Enter a phone number:</label><br><br>
      <input type="tel" id="phone" name="phone" value='+880' pattern="\+[0-9]{13}" required><br><br>
      <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    </form>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`pattern`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Regular Expression(like `\+[0-9]{13}`) ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ **`pattern`** Attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá (text, date, search, url, tel, email, and password) Input Field ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡•§
    
    ### <ins>***Range Input Fields***</ins> :
    
    **`<input type="range">`** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Number ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Range Control ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Controller ‡¶è‡¶∞ Default Value ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá 0 ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 100. ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`min`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`max`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Minimum ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Maximum Value ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`step`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Number Value ‡¶ï‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ Example :
    
    ```html
    <form action="#">
      <label for="vol">Volume (between 0 and 50):</label>
      <input type="range" id="vol" name="vol" min="0" max="50" step="10">
      <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    </form>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>***URL Input Fields***</ins> :
    
    **`<input type="url">`**  ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü User Input ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá URL Address ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ Depend ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá URL Field Automatically Validated ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá User ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® Form Submit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <form action="#">
      <label for="fb">Add your Facebook URL:</label>
      <input type="url" id="fb" name="fb">
      <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    </form>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>***Date Input Fields***</ins> :
    
    **`<input type="date">`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Date Input ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Example :
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    <body>
    <h2>Date Field</h2>
    <form action="#">
      <label for="birthday">Birthday:</label>
      <input type="date" id="birthday" name="birthday">
      <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    </form>
    <p><strong>Note:</strong> type="date" is not supported in Internet Explorer 11.</p>
    </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`min`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`max`** Attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Date Input Field ‡¶è Minimum ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Maximum Date ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<body>
    			<h2>Date Field Restrictions</h2>
    			<form action="#">
    			  <label for="datemin">Enter a date after 2000-01-01:</label>
    			  <input type="date" id="datemin" name="datemin" min="2000-01-02"><br><br>
    			
    			  <label for="datemax">Enter a date before 1980-01-01:</label>
    			  <input type="date" id="datemax" name="datemax" max="1979-12-31"><br><br>
    			  
    			  <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    			</form>
    			<p><strong>Note:</strong> type="date" is not supported in Internet Explorer 11.</p>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>***Time input fields***</ins> :
    
    **`<input type="time">`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Time Input ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Example :
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<body>
    		<h1>Show a Time Input Control</h1>
    		<form action="#">
    		  <label for="appt">Select a time:</label>
    		  <input type="time" id="appt" name="appt">
    		  <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    		</form>
    		<p><strong>Note:</strong> type="time" is not supported in Internet Explorer 11.</p>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>***Datetime-local Field***</ins> :
    
    **`<input type="datetime-local">`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Date ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Time ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Input ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<body>
    		<h2>Local Date Field</h2>
    		<form action="#">
    		  <label for="birthdaytime">Birthday (date and time):</label>
    		  <input type="datetime-local" id="birthdaytime" name="birthdaytime">
    		  <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    		</form>
    		<p><strong>Note:</strong> type="datetime-local" is not supported in Internet Explorer 11.</p>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>***Color fields***</ins> :
    
    **`<input type="color">`**  ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Color Input ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    <body>
    
    <h2>Show a Color Picker</h2>
    
    <form>
      <label for="favcolor">Select your favorite color:</label>
      <input type="color" id="favcolor" name="favcolor" value="#ff0000">
      <input type="submit" value="Submit">
    </form>
    
    <p><b>Note:</b> type="color" is not supported in Internet Explorer 11.</p>
    
    </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>***Image input fields***</ins> :
    
    **`<input type="image">`**  ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Image Button ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example : 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<body>
    		<h2>Display an Image as the Submit button</h2>
    		<form action="#">
    		  <label for="fname">First name: </label>
    		  <input type="text" id="fname" name="fname"><br><br>
    		  <label for="lname">Last name: </label>
    		  <input type="text" id="lname" name="lname"><br><br>
    		  <input type="image" src="img_submit.gif" alt="Submit" width="48" height="48">
    		</form>
    		<p><b>Note:</b> The input type="image" sends the X and Y coordinates of the click that activated the image button.</p>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>***Search input fields***</ins> :
    
    **`<input type="search">`** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Search Field ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example : 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<body>
    		<h2>Search Field</h2>
    		<form action="#">
    		  <label for="gsearch">Search Google:</label>
    		  <input type="search" id="gsearch" name="gsearch">
    		</form>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>***Html Progress Element***</ins> :
    
    Html **`<progress>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Task ‡¶è‡¶∞ Progress ‡¶ï‡¶§‡¶ü‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<body>
    		<h1>The progress element</h1>
    		<label for="file">Downloading progress:</label>
    		<progress id="file" value="50" max="100"> </progress>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ---
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶®  ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á , Html Head Element ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡•§
    
    HTML **`<head>`** Element ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Metadata Container ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü **`<html>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`<body>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡•§ Metadata ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Information ‡¶Ø‡¶æ SEO(Search Engine Optimization) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá‡•§ HTML **`<head>`** Element, HTML Document ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ Page Load ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü Display ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ HTML Head ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ HTML Document ‡¶è‡¶∞ Meta Data(document title, character set, styles, links, scripts, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç other meta information) ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ 
    
    Head ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá Tag ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É
    
    - **`<title>`**
    - **`<style>`**
    - **`<meta>`**
    - **`<link>`**
    - **`<script>`**
    - **`<base>`**
    
    ### <ins>***HTML Title Element***</ins> :
    
    Html **`<title>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Title ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Title ‡¶ü‡¶ø Show ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ Title Bar ‡¶è ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ Page Tab ‡¶è‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML Document ‡¶è Title Element ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ Required ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Search Engine Optimization(SEO) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Page Title ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§ Page Title ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Search Engine Algorithm ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶®‡ßá‡ßü Google Search Result ‡¶è  Order List ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Search Engine Result Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü‡¶ì Title ‡¶ü‡¶æ Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    <head>
      <title>A Meaningful Page Title</title>
    </head>
    <body>
    
    The content of the document......
    
    </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>***HTML Style Element***</ins> :
    
    **`<style>`** Element ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Single Page Information Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ Internal CSS ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á Element ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    <head>
      <title>Page Title</title>
      <style>
        body {background-color: powderblue;}
        h1 {color: red;}
        p {color: blue;}
      </style>
    </head>  
    <body>
      <h1>This is a Heading</h1>
      <p>This is a paragraph.</p>
    </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>***HTML Link Element***</ins> :
    
    Html **`<link>`** Element ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Current File ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç External File ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Relation ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á **`<link>`** element ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü External CSS Stylesheet Link ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ Example
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<head>
    	  <title>Page Title</title>
    	  <link rel="stylesheet" href="./mystyle.css">
    	</head>
    	<body>
    		<h1>This is a Heading</h1>
    		<p>This is a paragraph.</p>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`<link>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ HTML Favicon ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§Favicon ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Small Image ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Display ‡¶π‡ßü Browser Tab ‡¶è Title ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∂‡ßá‡•§ Web Page ‡¶è Favicon ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá Favicon Image ‡¶ü‡¶æ Root Directory ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ Image Folder ‡¶è ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Favicon Image ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Common Name ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É ‚Äúfavcion.ico‚Äù. Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<head>
    	  <title>My Page Title</title>
    	  <link rel="icon" type="image/x-icon" href="./images/favicon.ico">
    	</head>
    	<body>
    		<h1>This is a Heading</h1>
    		<p>This is a paragraph.</p>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    > üí° <ins>***Note***</ins> : Favicon File Format ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Browser Support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
    

    
    ### <ins>***HTML Script Element***</ins> :
    
    Html **`<script>`** Element ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü Client Side JavaScript ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ **`<script>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ JavaScript Code ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Current File ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá External JavaScript File ‡¶è‡¶∞ Relation ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<head>
    	  <title>Page Title</title>
    	  <script>
    		  function myFunction() {
    		    document.getElementById("demo").innerHTML = "Hello JavaScript!";
    		  }
    	  </script>
    	</head>
    	<body>
    		<h1>My Web Page</h1>
    		<p id="demo">A Paragraph</p>
    		<button type="button" onclick="myFunction()">Try it</button>
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>***HTML Base Element***</ins> :
    
    Html **`<base>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Base URL ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ Target ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Relative URL ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Element ‡¶è ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶∂‡¶á **`herf`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`target`** Attribute ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    <head>
      <base href="https://www.w3schools.com/" target="_blank">
    </head>
    <body>
      <h1>The base element</h1>
      <p><a href="tags/tag_base.asp">HTML base tag</a> - Notice that the link opens in a new window, even if it has no target="_blank" attribute. This is because the target attribute of the base element is set to "_blank".</p>
    
    </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    > üí° <ins>***Note***</ins> : ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Document ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶á **`<base>`** Element ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    
    
    ### <ins>***HTML Meta Element***</ins> :
    
    Html **`<meta>`** Element ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü character set, page description, keywords, author name of the document, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç viewport settings ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§  Metadata ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Information ‡¶Ø‡¶æ SEO(Search Engine Optimization) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá‡•§ Metadata Browser Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá display ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ 
    
    ***Define the character set used :***
    
    > \<meta¬†charset="UTF-8">
    
    ***Define keywords for search engines :***
    
    > \<meta¬†name="keywords"¬†content="HTML, CSS, JavaScript">
    
    ***Define a description of your web page :***
    
    > \<meta¬†name="description"¬†content="Free Web tutorials">
    
    ***Define the author of a page :***
    
    > \<meta¬†name="author"¬†content="John Doe">
    
    ***Refresh document every 30 seconds :***
    
    > \<meta¬†http-equiv="refresh"¬†content="30">
    
    ***Setting the viewport to make your website look good on all devices :***
    
    > \<meta¬†name="viewport"¬†content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    
     ***Define the Google BOT Follow or Unfollow your Content Links :***
    
    > \<meta¬†name="robots"¬†content="index, follow">
    
    Example :
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    	<head>
    	  <meta charset="UTF-8">
    	  <meta name="description" content="Free Web tutorials">
    	  <meta name="keywords" content="HTML, CSS, JavaScript">
    	  <meta name="author" content="Shahid">
    	  <meta¬†name="robots"¬†content="index, follow">
    	  <meta¬†name="viewport"¬†content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    	</head>
    	<body>
    	    Content......
    	</body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>***Setting the Viewport***</ins> :
    
    Viewport ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ Visible Area ‡¶Ø‡¶æ User ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ Device ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Computer Screen ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá Area ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßú ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Mobile ‡¶¨‡¶æ Tablet ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá Area ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Area ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® Device ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ **`<meta>`** ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø:
    
    > **\<meta¬†name="viewport"¬†content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">**
    
    ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ü‡¶ø Browser ‡¶ï‡ßá Instruction ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ Dimension ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Scaling Control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ **width=device-width** ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ü‡¶ø  Device ‡¶è‡¶∞ Screen-Width ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá Webpage ‡¶è‡¶∞ Width Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ **initial-scale=1.0** ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ü‡¶ø Browser ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® Page Load ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Initial Zoom Level Set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
    
    Example :
    
    **Without the viewport meta tag** :
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    <head>
        <title>Without Viewport</title>
    </head>
    <body>
        <h1>Without Viewport</h1>
      <img src="./images/photo.jpeg" alt="Lake Image" width="500" height="350">
      <p style="text-align:justify;"> Lorem Ipsum is simply dummy text of the printing and typesetting industry. Lorem Ipsum has been the industry's standard dummy text ever since the 1500s, when an unknown printer took a galley of type and scrambled it to make a type specimen book. It has survived not only five centuries, but also the leap into electronic typesetting, remaining essentially unchanged. It was popularised in the 1960s with the release of Letraset sheets containing Lorem Ipsum passages, and more recently with desktop publishing software like Aldus PageMaker including versions of Lorem Ipsum.</p>
    </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    **With the viewport meta tag** :
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    <head>
      <meta charset="UTF-8">
      <title>With Viewport</title>
      <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0"/>
      <style>
        img{
            max-width: 100%;
            height: auto;
        }
      </style>
    </head>
    <body>
        <h1>With Viewport</h1>
      <img src="./images/photo.jpeg" alt="Lake Image" width="500" height="350">
      <p style="text-align:justify;"> Lorem Ipsum is simply dummy text of the printing and typesetting industry. Lorem Ipsum has been the industry's standard dummy text ever since the 1500s, when an unknown printer took a galley of type and scrambled it to make a type specimen book. It has survived not only five centuries, but also the leap into electronic typesetting, remaining essentially unchanged. It was popularised in the 1960s with the release of Letraset sheets containing Lorem Ipsum passages, and more recently with desktop publishing software like Aldus PageMaker including versions of Lorem Ipsum.</p>
    </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶®  ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á , Html Layout ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡•§
    
    HTML Layout ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá Web Page ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Well-Mannered, Well-Structured ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Responsive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé HTML Layout ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Web Page ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Website ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü Web Page Layout ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï Important ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Part, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Website ‡¶ï‡ßá Professional Look ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Life ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∏ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶∂‡¶á Layout ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá‡•§ HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ HTML Layout ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ HTML Layout ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® HTML Layout Element ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá HTML Semantic(elements with a meaning) Element ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Element ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ There are: 
    
    ![https://www.w3schools.com/html/img_sem_elements.gif](https://www.w3schools.com/html/img_sem_elements.gif)
    
    - **`<header>`**
    - **`<nav>`**
    - **`<section>`**
    - **`<article>`**
    - **`<aside>`**
    - **`<footer>`**
    - **`<details>`** & **`<summary>`**
    - **`<main>`**
    - **`<time>`**
    - **`<figure>`** & **`<figcaption>`**
    
    ### <ins>*HTML Header Element*</ins> :
    
    **`<header>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Document ‡¶è‡¶∞ Header Section ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ Header ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Introductory Content, Heading Element, Logo or Icon For The Webpage, and Authorship Information ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Example :
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
           <title>HTML Head Element</title>
      </head>
      <body>
          <article>
             <header>
    ¬†¬†¬†         <h1>A heading here</h1>
                <p>Posted by John Doe</p>
    			      <p>Some additional information here</p>
             </header>
                <p>Lorem Ipsum dolor set amet....</p>
          </article>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>*HTML Nav Element*</ins> :
    
    **`<nav>`** Element Navigation Links ‡¶è‡¶∞ Main Block Container ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Section ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Current Page Or Other Pages ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Link Contain ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Example: 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
           <title>HTML Nav Element</title>
      </head>
      <body>
        <nav style="background-color:skyblue; text-align:center">
          <h1 style="text-align: center;">Navgation Links</h1>
           <a href="#">Home </a>|
           <a href="#">Services </a> |
           <a href="#">About </a>|
           <a href="#">Gallery </a>|
           <a href="#">Contact </a>
        </nav>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`text-align`** CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ Part. Navigation ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá CSS Notes ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ 
    
    ### <ins>*HTML Section Element*</ins> :
    
    **`<section>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Element ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Related Element Content ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá Group ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá text, images, tables, videos ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
           <title>HTML Section Element</title>
      </head>
      <body>
        <section style="background-color:#ff7f50; border: 2px solid black;">
     	    <h1>Section A</h1>
          <p>Lorem Ipsum is simply dummy text of the printing and typesetting industry. Lorem Ipsum has been the industry's standard dummy text ever since the 1500s, when an unknown printer took a galley of type and scrambled it to make a type specimen book.</p>
        </section>
         <br>
        <section style="background-color:#ff7f50; border: 2px solid black;">
          <h1>Section B</h1>
          <p>Lorem Ipsum is simply dummy text of the printing and typesetting industry. Lorem Ipsum has been the industry's standard dummy text ever since the 1500s, when an unknown printer took a galley of type and scrambled it to make a type specimen book.</p>
        </section>
     </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`background-color`** , **`border`** ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ Part. Section Part ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá CSS Notes ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    
    ### <ins>*HTML Article Element*</ins> :

    **`<article>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Section ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Article Related ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Group ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® Blog Post, Big Story, Forum Posts, User Comments, Product Cards, Newspaper Articles ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§ Example : 
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
           <title>HTML Article Element</title>
      </head>
      <body>
         <h1>The article element</h1>
         <article style="border:2px solid black;">
            <h2>Google Chrome</h2>
            <p>Google Chrome is a web browser developed by Google, released in 2008. Chrome is the world's most popular web browser today!</p>
         </article>
         <br>
        <article style="border:2px solid black;">
          <h2>Mozilla Firefox</h2>
          <p>Mozilla Firefox is an open-source web browser developed by Mozilla. Firefox has been the second most popular web browser since January, 2018.        </p>
        </article>
         <br>
        <article style="border:2px solid black;">
          <h2>Microsoft Edge</h2>
          <p>Microsoft Edge is a web browser developed by Microsoft, released in 2015. Microsoft Edge replaced Internet Explorer.</p>
        </article>
    </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>*HTML Aside Element*</ins> :
    
    **`<aside>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Section ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Sidebar ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Section ‡¶è ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Main Content Or Primary Content ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
           <title>HTML Aside Element</title>
      </head>
      <body>
         <aside style="background-color:skyblue; border: 1px solid ">
           <h4>Most Visited Post</h4>
           <ul>
              <li><a href="#">HTML Tutorial</a> </li> 
              <li><a href="#">CSS Tutorial</a> </li>
              <li><a href="#">Javascript Tutorial</a> </li>
           </ul>
           <h4> Top 5 Post</h4>
           <ul>
             <li><a href="#">HTML Tutorial</a> </li> 
             <li><a href="#">CSS Tutorial</a> </li>
             <li><a href="#">Javascript Tutorial</a> </li>
             <li><a href="#">PHP Tutorial</a> </li>
             <li><a href="#">SQL Tutorial</a> </li>
          </ul>
        </aside>
    </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>*HTML Footer Element*</ins> :
    
    **`<footer>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Web Page ‡¶è‡¶∞ Footer ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ Define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á  Section ‡¶è ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ Author Information, Copyright Information, Contact Information, Sitemap, Back to Top Links, Related Documents ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
           <title>HTML Footer Element</title>
      </head>
      <body>
        <footer style="background-color:skyblue; text-align: center;">
    	   <p>Author: Shahidul Islam</p>
           <p><a href="mailto:shahid@example.com">shahid@example.com</a></p>
    	   <p>&copy; Copyright 2023.</p>
        </footer>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>*HTML Details & Summary Element*</ins> :
    
    **`<details>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Element ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Toggle List ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Details Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ Data ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Show ‡¶¨‡¶æ Hide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ **`<details>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü‡ßá‡¶∞ Additional Details Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ **`<summary>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **`<details>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ Visible Heading ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
           <title>HTML Details and Summary Element</title>
      </head>
      <body>
         <details>
            <summary>Learn about HTML Details Element</summary>
            <p>Lorem Ipsum is simply dummy text of the printing and typesetting industry. Lorem Ipsum has been the industry's standard dummy text ever since the 1500s, when an unknown printer took a galley of type and scrambled it to make a type specimen book. </p> 
         </details>
         <details>
            <summary>Learn about HTML Summary Element</summary>
            <p>Lorem Ipsum is simply dummy text of the printing and typesetting industry. Lorem Ipsum has been the industry's standard dummy text ever since the 1500s, when an unknown printer took a galley of type and scrambled it to make a type specimen book. </p> 
         </details>
    </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>*HTML Main Element*</ins> :
    
    **`<main>`** Element ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Document ‡¶è‡¶∞ Main Content ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`<main>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Document ‡¶è‡¶∞ **`<article>`** **`<aside>`** **`<section>`** ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Group ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **`<main>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶á Element ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ Parent Section ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø Document ‡¶è  **`<main>`** Element ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø‡•§ Example :
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
           <title>HTML Main Element</title>
      </head>
      <body>
         <main>
            <h1>Most Popular Browsers</h1>
            <p>Chrome, Firefox, and Edge are the most used browsers today.</p>
            <article>
                <h2>Google Chrome</h2>
                <p>Google Chrome is a web browser developed by Google, released in 2008. Chrome is the world's most popular web browser today!</p>
            </article>
            <article>
                <h2>Mozilla Firefox</h2>
                <p>Mozilla Firefox is an open-source web browser developed by Mozilla. Firefox has been the second most popular web browser since January, 2018.</p>
            </article>
            <article>
                <h2>Microsoft Edge</h2>
                <p>Microsoft Edge is a web browser developed by Microsoft, released in 2015. Microsoft Edge replaced Internet Explorer.</p>
            </article>
        </main>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>*HTML Time Element*</ins> :
    
    **`<time>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Date ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Time ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø 24 Hours Clock ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç HTML Gregorian Calendar ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Date Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ Task Schedule ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Search Engine ‡¶è Smart Search Result Display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ **`datetime`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Date ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Time ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
           <title>HTML Time Element</title>
      </head>
    <body>
      <h1>The time element</h1>
      <p>We open our shop at <time>09:00</time> am.</p>  
      <p>The business meeting is scheduled on <time datetime="2009-02-18">next wednesday</time>.</p>  
      <p>The wedding of Salman's sister was scheduled  at <time datetime="2014-11-19 T0 7:00-09:00">7pm last wednesday </time>.</p>  
    </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ### <ins>*HTML figure & figcaption Element*</ins> :
    
    **`<figure>`** Element ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® Web Page ‡¶è Group of Photo Or Diagrams, Or Code Listing Mark Up ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá **`<figcaption>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Photo Or Diagrams ‡¶è‡¶∞ Caption Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example :
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
       <head>
           <title> HTML Figure and Figcaption Element </title>
      </head>
      <body>
         <figure>
            <img src="pic_trulli.jpg" alt="Trulli" style="width:100%">
            <figcaption>Fig.1 - Trulli, Puglia, Italy.</figcaption>
         </figure>
    
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ## Non Semantic Element :
    
    HTML ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ø Non Semantic Element ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É <div> ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç <span> Tag.
    
    ### <ins>*HTML Div Element*</ins>:
    
    **`<div>`** Element ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü HTML Document ‡¶è‡¶∞ Section ‡¶¨‡¶æ Division ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ **`<div>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Elements Of Container ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶§‡ßá CSS ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
      <head>
         <title> HTML Div Element </title>
         <style>
           .myDiv {
              border: 5px outset red;
              background-color: lightblue;    
              text-align: center;
           }
        </style>
      </head>
      <body>
        <h1>The div element</h1>
        <div class="myDiv">
           <h2>This is a heading in a div element</h2>
            <p>This is some text in a div element.</p>
        </div>
       <p>This is some text outside the div element.</p>
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    **`<div>`** Tag ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü Group Of HTML Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá CSS Apply ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Set Of Paragraph ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Div ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã Paragraph ‡¶è‡¶∞ Font Style ‡¶¨‡¶æ Other Style ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ HTML **`<div>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Block Element. 
    
    ### HTML Span Element:
    
    **`<span>`** Tag ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Inline Container,‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Text ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡ßá Mark ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Easily **`id`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`class`** Attribute Add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá CSS Style ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Example:
    
    ```html
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
       <head>
           <title> HTML Figure and Figcaption Element </title>
      </head>
      <body>
          <h1>The span element</h1>
           <p>My mother has <span style="color:blue;font-weight:bold">blue</span> eyes and my father has <span style="color:red;font-weight:bold">red</span> eyes.</p>
    
      </body>
    </html>
    ```
    
    ## HTML Div Tag ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Span Tag ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶•‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶≤ :
    
    | Div Tag | Span Tag |
    | --- | --- |
    | HTML div ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø¬†block¬†element. | HTML span ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø¬†inline¬†element | 
    | Html div Element ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶¨‡ßú Section ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§     | Html span Element ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßá Style ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§      |
    
    ## HTML Layout Techniques:
    
    ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ Different Techniques ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ HTML Layout ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Multicolumn Layout ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø Technique ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ/‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ Techniques ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É
    
    - CSS framework
    - CSS float property
    - CSS flexbox
    - CSS grid
    
    ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá CSS Notes ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
    
    ---
    
- ## Html Responsive Web Design ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£?
    
    Responsive Web Design ‡¶π‡¶≤ HTML ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç CSS ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Automatically ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Website ‡¶ï‡ßá Resize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ, Shrink ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ Enlarge ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∏‡ßá (desktops, tablets, and phones) ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ Website ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ Device ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Responsive ‡¶ì ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ 
    
    ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø Website Responsive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Document ‡¶è‡¶∞ Head Element ‡¶è ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á (\<meta¬†name="viewport"¬†content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">) ‡¶è‡¶á Line ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá Responsive Code ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ì Responsiveness  ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ 
    
- ## ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶®  ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶á, Html  Entities & Symbols ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡•§
    
    HTML Character Entities Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü HTML Reserved Characters Replacement ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá Keyboard ‡¶è ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® Entities ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§ HTML ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Reserved Characters ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§  ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Less Than(<) Or Greater Than (>) Symbol Use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á HTML Document ‡¶è ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã HTML Reserved Characters. ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá HTML Entities ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá icons, geometric shapes, mathematical operators ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Web Page ‡¶è‡•§
    
    HTML Entities Syntax:  **`&entity_name;`**  Or **`&#entity_number;`**
    
    ***‡¶∏‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ HTML Entities ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡¶É***
    
    ![HTML Entities.png](./document-Images/HTML_Entities.png)
    
    ***‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Mathematical Symbols ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã HTML Support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶É***
    
    ![HTML Mathmatical Symbol.png](./document-Images/HTML_Mathmatical_Symbol.png)
    
- ## *** ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Html Style Tips ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§ ***
    1. ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü Document ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá Document Type ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ 
    
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        ```
    
    2. Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ 
    
        **Good:**
        
        ```html
        <body>
          <p>This is a paragraph.</p>
        </body>
        ```
        
        **Bad:**
        
        ```html
        <BODY>
            <P>This is a paragraph.</P>
        </BODY>
        ```
    
    3. ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü Html Element Close ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ 
    
        **Good:**
        
        ```html
        <hr/>
        <section>
          <p>This is a paragraph.</p>
          <p>This is a paragraph.</p>
        </section>
        ```
        
        **Bad:**
        
        ```html
        <hr>
        <section>
          <p>This is a paragraph.
          <p>This is a paragraph.
        </section>
        ```
    
    4. ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ì ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
        
        **Good:**
        
        ```html
        <a href="https://www.w3schools.com/html/">Visit our HTML tutorial</a>
        ```
        
        **Bad:**
        
        ```html
        <a HREF="https://www.w3schools.com/html/">Visit our HTML tutorial</a>
        ```
        
    5. ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü Attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ Value ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá Quote(‚Äù ‚Äù) ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶π‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ 
        
        **Good:**
        
        ```html
        <table class="striped">
        ```
        
        **Bad:**
        
        ```html
        <table class=striped>
        ```
    
    6. Image ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶∂‡¶á **`alt`** Attribute ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`width`** ‡¶ì **`height`** Attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ 
    
        **Good:**
        
        ```html
        <img src=""./flower.jpg" alt="Flower" style="width:128px;height:128px">
        ```
        
        **Bad:**
        
        ```html
        <img src="./flower.jpg">
        ```
    
    7. Attribute ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü Attribute name ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ value Equal (=) ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶π‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ù‡ßá ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Å‡¶ï‡¶æ Space ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ 
    
        **Good:**
        
        ```html
        <link rel="stylesheet" href="styles.css">
        ```
        
        **Bad:**
        
        ```html
        <link rel = "stylesheet" href = "styles.css">
        ```
    
    8. ‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶®‡ßã **`<title>`** Element Skip ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ Search Engine ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§ 
    
        ```html
        <title>HTML Style Guide and Coding Conventions</title>
        ```
    
    9. ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü **`<html>`** Element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá **`lang`** Attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Web Page ‡¶è Language ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Search Engine ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Browser ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ 
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html lang="en-us">
          <head>
            <title>Page Title</title>
          </head>
          <body>
            <h1>This is a heading</h1>
            <p>This is a paragraph.</p>
          </body>
        </html>
        ```
        
    10. ‡¶∏‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Search Engine Indexing ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá Language ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Character Encoding **`<meta charset=‚Äùcharset‚Äù>`** ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡•§ 
        
        ```html
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html lang="en-us">
        <head>
          <meta charset="UTF-8">
          <title>Page Title</title>
        </head>
        ```
